{ useState, useEffect, useRef, useCallback } from 'react';\n\ninterface UseVoiceOptions {\n  onCommand?: (cmd: string) => void;\n  onDigits?: (digits: string) => void;\n  autoStart?: boolean;\n '2',\n  'three': '3', 'tree': '3',\n  'four': '4', 'for': '4',\n  'five': '5',\n  'six': '6',\n  'seven': '7',\n  'eight': '8', 'ate': '8',\n  'nine': '9',\n};\n\nexport const extractDigits = (text: string): string => {\n  const words = text.toLowerCase().split(/[\\s,.\\-]+/);\n  let digits = '';\n  for (const word of words) {\n    if (WORD_TO_DIGIT[word]) digits += WORD_TO_DIGIT[word];\n    else e.error !== 'aborted') {\n        console.error('Speech error:', e.error);\n      }\n    };\n\n    rec.onend = () => {\n      if (isListeningRef.current && !isPaused) {\n        setTimeout(() => { try { rec.start(); } catch (e) {} }, 100);\n      }\n    };\n\n    recRef.current = rec;\n    \n    if (autoStart) {\n      setIsListening(true);\n      try { rec.start(); } catch (e) {}\n    }\n\n setIsSpeaking(false);\n  }, []);\n\n  const pause = useCallback(() => {\n    setIsPaused(true);\n    try { recRef.current?.stop(); } catch (e) {}\n  }, []);\n\n  const resume = useCallback(() => {\n
